Http::FilterTrailersStatus::Continue;\n   311→}\n   312→\n   313→Http::Filter1xxHeadersStatus Filter::encode1xxHeaders(Http::ResponseHeaderMap&) {\n   314→  return Filters::Common::MutationRules::CheckOperation operation, absl::string_view key,\n   394→    absl::string_view value) const {\n   395→  if (config_->validateMutations() &&   402→\n   403→void Filter::onComplete(Filters::Common::ExtAuthz::ResponsePtr&& response) {\n   404→  state_ = State::Complete;\n   405→  using Filters::Common::ExtAuthz::CheckStatus;\n   406→  Stats::StatName empty_stat_name;\n   407→\n   408→  if (!response->dynamic_metadata.fields().empty()) {\n   409→    if (!config_->enableDynamicMetadataIngestion()) {\n   410→ Ignoring...\",\n   413→                       *decoder_callbacks_);\n   414→      stats_.ignored_dynamic_metadata_.inc();\n   415→    } else {\n   416→      // Add duration of call to dynamic metadata if applicable\n   417→      if (start_time_.has_value() && response->status == CheckStatus::OK) {\n   418→        ProtobufWkt::Value ext_authz_duration_value;\n   419→        auto duration =\n   420→            decoder_callbacks_->dispatcher().timeSource().monotonicTime() - start_time_.value();\n   421→        ext_authz_duration_value.set_number_value(\n   422→            std::chrono::duration_cast<std::chrono::milliseconds>(duration).count());\n   423→        (*response->dynamic_metadata.mutable_fields())[\"ext_authz_duration\"] =\n   424→            ext_authz_duration_value;\n   425→      }\n   426→      decoder_callbacks_->streamInfo().setDynamicMetadata(\"envoy.filters.http.ext_authz\",\n   427→                                                          response->dynamic_metadata);\n   428→    }\n   429→  }\n   430→\n   431→  switch (response->status) {\n   432→  case CheckStatus::OK: {\n   433→    // Any changes to request headers or query parameters can affect how the request is going to be\n   434→    // routed. If we are changing the headers we also need to clear the route\n   435→    // cache.\n   436→    if (config_->clearRouteCache() &&\n   437→        (!response->headers_to_set.empty() || !response->headers_to_append.empty() ||\n   438→         !response->headers_to_remove.empty() || !response->query_parameters_to_set.empty() ||\n   439→         !response->query_parameters_to_remove.empty())) {\n   440→      ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(debug, \"ext_authz is clearing route cache\", *decoder_callbacks_);\n   441→ request:\", *decoder_callbacks_);\n   446→    for (const auto& [key, value] : response->headers_to_set) {\n   447→      CheckResult check_result = validateAndCheckDecoderHeaderMutation(\n   448→          Filters::Common::MutationRules::CheckOperation::SET, key, value);\n   449→      switch (check_result) {\n   450→      case CheckResult::OK:\n   451→        ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"'{}':'{}'\", *decoder_callbacks_, key, value);\n   452→        request_headers_->setCopy(Http::LowerCaseString(key), value);\n   453→        break;\n   454→      case CheckResult::IGNORE:\n   455→        ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"Ignoring invalid header to set '{}':'{}'.\", *decoder_callbacks_,\n   456→                         key, value);\n   457→        break;\n   458→      case CheckResult::FAIL:\n   459→        ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"Rejecting invalid header to set '{}':'{}'.\", *decoder_callbacks_,\n   460→                         key, value);\n   461→        rejectResponse();\n   462→        return;\n   463→      }\n   464→    }\n   465→    for (const auto& [key, value] : response->headers_to_add) {\n   466→      CheckResult check_result = validateAndCheckDecoderHeaderMutation(\n   467→          Filters::Common::MutationRules::CheckOperation::SET, key, value);\n   468→      switch (check_result) {\n   469→      case CheckResult::OK:\n   470→        ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"'{}':'{}'\", *decoder_callbacks_, key, value);\n   471→        request_headers_->addCopy(Http::LowerCaseString(key), value);\n   472→        break;\n   473→      case CheckResult::IGNORE:\n   474→        ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"Ignoring invalid header to add '{}':'{}'.\", *decoder_callbacks_,\n   475→                         key, value);\n   476→        break;\n   477→      case CheckResult::FAIL:\n   478→        ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"Rejecting invalid header to add '{}':'{}'.\", *decoder_callbacks_,\n   479→                         key, value);\n   480→        rejectResponse();\n   481→        return;\n   482→      }\n   483→    }\n   484→    for (const auto& [key, value] : response->headers_to_append) {\n   485→      CheckResult check_result = validateAndCheckDecoderHeaderMutation(\n   486→          Filters::Common::MutationRules::CheckOperation::APPEND, key, value);\n   487→      switch (check_result) {\n   488→      case CheckResult::OK: {\n   489→        ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"'{}':'{}'\", *decoder_callbacks_, key, value);\n   490→        Http::LowerCaseString lowercase_key(key);\n   491→        const auto header_to_modify = request_headers_->get(lowercase_key);\n   492→        // TODO(dio): Add a flag to allow appending non-existent headers, without setting it\n   493→        // first (via `headers_to_add`). For example, given:\n   494→        // 1. Original headers {\"original\": \"true\"}\n   495→        // 2. Response headers from the authorization servers {{\"append\": \"1\"}, {\"append\":\n   496→        // \"2\"}}\n   497→        //\n   498→        // Currently it is not possible to add {{\"append\": \"1\"}, {\"append\": \"2\"}} (the\n   499→        // intended combined headers: {{\"original\": \"true\"}, {\"append\": \"1\"}, {\"append\":\n   500→        // \"2\"}}) to the request to upstream server by only sets `headers_to_append`.\n   501→        if (!header_to_modify.empty()) {\n   502→          ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"'{}':'{}'\", *decoder_callbacks_, key, value);\n   503→          // The current behavior of appending is by combining entries with the same key,\n   504→          // into one entry. The value of that combined entry is separated by \",\".\n   505→          // TODO(dio): Consider to use addCopy instead.\n   506→          request_headers_->appendCopy(lowercase_key, value);\n   507→        }\n   508→        break;\n   509→      }\n   510→      case CheckResult::IGNORE:\n   511→        ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"Ignoring invalid header to append '{}':'{}'.\", *decoder_callbacks_,\n   512→                         key, value);\n   513→        break;\n   514→      case CheckResult::FAIL:\n   515→        ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"Rejecting invalid header to append '{}':'{}'.\",\n   516→                         *decoder_callbacks_, key, value);\n   517→        rejectResponse();\n   518→        return;\n   519→      }\n   520→    }\n   521→\n   522→    ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace,\n   523→                     \"ext_authz filter removed header(s) from the request:\", *decoder_callbacks_);\n   524→    for (const auto& key : response->headers_to_remove) {\n   525→      // If the response contains an invalid header to remove, it's the same as trying to remove a\n   526→      // header that doesn't exist, so just ignore it.\n   527→      if (config_->validateMutations() && !Http::HeaderUtility::headerNameIsValid(key)) {\n   528→        ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"Ignoring invalid header removal '{}'.\", *decoder_callbacks_, key);\n   529→        continue;\n   530→      }\n   531→      // We don't allow removing any :-prefixed headers, nor Host, as removing them would make the\n   532→      // request malformed. checkDecoderHeaderMutation also performs this check, !Http::HeaderUtility::isRemovableHeader(key)) {\n   536→        ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"Ignoring invalid header removal '{}'.\", *decoder_callbacks_, key);\n   537→        continue;\n   538→       ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"Rejecting disallowed header removal '{}'.\", *decoder_callbacks_,\n   553→                         key);\n   554→        rejectResponse();\n   555→        return;\n   556→      }\n   557→    }\n   558→\n   559→    if (!response->response_headers_to_add.empty()) {\n   560→      ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"ext_authz filter saving {} header(s) to add to the response:\",\n   561→                       *decoder_callbacks_, response->response_headers_to_add.size());\n   562→      for (const auto& [key, value] : response->response_headers_to_add) {\n   563→        if (config_->validateMutations() && (!Http::HeaderUtility::headerNameIsValid(key) ||\n   564→                                             !Http::HeaderUtility::headerValueIsValid(value))) {\n          response->response_headers_to_add_if_absent.end()};\n   606→    }\n   607→\n   608→    if (!response->response_headers_to_overwrite_if_exists.empty()) {\n   609→      ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace,                      response->response_headers_to_overwrite_if_exists.end()};\n   624→    }\n   625→\n   626→    absl::optional<Http::Utility::QueryParamsMulti> modified_query_parameters;\n   627→ modified_query_parameters->replaceQueryString(request_headers_->Path()->value());\n   664→      ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(\n   665→          trace, \"ext_authz filter modified query parameter(s), using new 692→                                               empty_stat_name,\n   693→                                               empty_stat_name,\n   694→                                               empty_stat_name,\n   695→                                               empty_stat_name,\n   696→                                               false};\n   697→        config_->httpContext().codeStats().chargeResponseStat(info, false);\n   698→      }\n   699→    }\n   700→\n   701→    // Check headers are valid.\n   702→    if (config_->validateMutations()) {\n   703→      for (const auto& [key, value] : response->headers_to_set) {\n   704→        if (!Http::HeaderUtility::headerNameIsValid(key) ||\n   705→            !Http::HeaderUtility::headerValueIsValid(value)) {\n   706→          ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"Rejected invalid header '{}':'{}'.\", *decoder_callbacks_, key,\n   707→                           value);\n   708→          rejectResponse();\n   709→          return;\n   710→        }\n   711→      }\n   712→    }\n   713→\n   714→    // setResponseFlag must be called before sendLocalReply\n   715→    decoder_callbacks_->streamInfo().setResponseFlag(\n   716→        StreamInfo::CoreResponseFlag::UnauthorizedExternalService);\n   717→    decoder_callbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n   718→        response->status_code, response->body,\n   719→        [&headers = response->headers_to_set,\n   720→         &callbacks = *decoder_callbacks_](Http::HeaderMap& response_headers) -> void {\n   721→          ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace,\n   722→                           \"ext_authz filter added header(s) to the local response:\", callbacks);\n   723→          // Firstly, remove all headers requested by the ext_authz filter, to ensure that they will\n   724→          // override existing headers.\n   725→          for (const auto& [key, _] : headers) {\n   726→            response_headers.remove(Http::LowerCaseString(key));\n   727→          }\n   728→          // Then set all of the requested headers, allowing the same header to be set multiple\n   729→          // times, e.g. `Set-Cookie`.\n   730→          for (const auto& [key, value] : headers) {\n   731→            ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \" '{}':'{}'\", callbacks, key, value);\n   732→   736→    break;\n   737→  }\n   738→\n   739→  case CheckStatus::Error: {\n   740→    if (cluster_) {\n   741→      config_->incCounter(cluster_->statsScope(), config_->ext_authz_error_);\n   742→    }\n   743→    stats_.error_.inc();\n   744→    if (config_->failureModeAllow()) {\n   745→      ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"ext_authz filter allowed the request with error\",\n   746→                       *decoder_callbacks_);\n   747→      stats_.failure_mode_allowed_.inc();\n   748→      if (cluster_) {\n   749→        config_->incCounter(cluster_->statsScope(), config_->ext_authz_failure_mode_allowed_);\n   750→      }\n   751→      if (config_->failureModeAllowHeaderAdd()) {\n   752→        request_headers_->addReferenceKey(\n   753→            Filters::Common::ExtAuthz::Headers::get().EnvoyAuthFailureModeAllowed, \"true\");\n   754→      }\n   755→      continueDecoding();\n   756→    } else {\n   757→      ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(\n   758→          trace, \"ext_authz filter rejected the request with an error. Response status code: {}\",\n   759→          *decoder_callbacks_, enumToInt(config_->statusOnError()));\n   760→      decoder_callbacks_->streamInfo().setResponseFlag(\n   761→          StreamInfo::CoreResponseFlag::UnauthorizedExternalService);\n   762→      decoder_callbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n   763→          config_->statusOnError(), EMPTY_STRING, nullptr, absl::nullopt,\n   764→          Filters::Common::ExtAuthz::ResponseCodeDetails::get().AuthzError);\n   765→    }\n   766→    break;\n   767→  }\n   768→  }\n   769→}\n   770→\n   771→void Filter::rejectResponse() {\n   772→  const Http::Code status = Http::Code::InternalServerError;\n   773→  ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"ext_authz filter invalidated the response. Response status code: {}\",\n   774→                   *decoder_callbacks_, enumToInt(status));\n   775→  if (cluster_) {\n   776→    config_->incCounter(cluster_->statsScope(),
